[30;1m298 | [0m[35mdef daterange(start, stop, step=1, inclusive=False):[0m
[30;1m299 | [0m[35m    """In the spirit of :func:`range` and :func:`xrange`, the `daterange`[0m
[30;1m300 | [0m[35m    generator that yields a sequence of :class:`~datetime.date`[0m
[30;1m301 | [0m[35m    objects, starting at *start*, incrementing by *step*, until *stop*[0m
